In [48]:
def get_detail(url):
    headers = random.choice(user_agent_list)
    #print(headers)
    HEADER1 = {
        'User-Agent': headers,
        'Accept-Language':'zh-CN,zh;q=0.9',
    }
    html = requests.get(url, headers=HEADER1)
    apparent_encoding = html.apparent_encoding
    html.encoding = apparent_encoding
    #print(html.text)
    return html.text
In [37]:
def get_ones(keyword):
    result_list = []
    url = "https://www.baidu.com/s?wd={}&tn=91003609_hao_pg".format(keyword)
    html = requests.get(url, headers=HEADER, timeout=10).text
    soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'lxml')
    items = soup.findAll('h3', class_='t')
    items_name = items[0].text
    items_url = items[0].find('a').attrs['href']
    item = [items_name, items_url]
    result_list.append(item)
    return result_list
In [4]:
def get_all(keyword):
    result_list = []
    idx = 0
    url = "https://www.baidu.com/s?wd={}&tn=91003609_hao_pg".format(keyword)
    while True:
        idx += 1
        # page_url = url.format(user, idx)
        if idx > 1:
            page_url = url
        else:
            page_url = url.format(keyword)

        try:
            html = requests.get(page_url, headers=HEADER, timeout=10).text
            # print("HTML"+html)
            soup = BeautifulSoup(html, 'lxml')

            items = soup.findAll('h3', class_='t')
            n = len(items)
            #print(n)
            for i in range(0, n):
                items_name = items[i].text
                items_url = items[i].find('a').attrs['href']
                #items_detail = get_detail(items_url)
                #item = [items_name, items_url,items_detail]
                item = [items_name, items_url]
                result_list.append(item)

            if '>&gt;</a>' not in html:
                break
            nextUrl = soup.find('div', id='page').children
            for urlItem in nextUrl:
                if urlItem.string == ">":
                    #print("oo"+urlItem.attrs['href'])
                    url = "https://www.baidu.com"+urlItem.attrs['href']
                    #print("hh"+url)

        except Exception as e:
            print(e)
    return result_list

words = []
file = open("Random_Input.txt")
while 1:
    line = file.readline()
    if not line:
        break
    words.append(line[6:-8])
In [39]:

for word in words:
    result = [0,0]
    if len(result)>0:
        result = get_ones(word)[0]
        print(result)
        Result.append(result)

import re
htmls = []
for item in Results:
    item_name = item[0]
    item_url = item[1]
    item_html = re.sub("[A-Za-z0-9\!\%\[\]\,\\<\>\/\.\=\"\\n\:\;\(\)\-\{\}\*\#\\\$\\\'\\\r\\t\+\&\\?\|\_\~ \__\\\\^^\\\]", "", item[2])
    htmls.append([item_name,item_url,item_html])

!function(){        require.async(["wiki-common:widget/lib/jquery/jquery"],function($){
            function openTagToggle(node) {
                if ($(node).hasClass("collapse")) {
                    $(node).removeClass("collapse");
                    $("#open-tag").css("height", '22px');
                } else {
                    $(node).addClass("collapse");
                    $("#open-tag").css("height", $("#open-tag-item").css("height"));
                }
            }
            if (parseInt($("#open-tag-item").css("height")) <= 30) {
                $('#open-tag-collapse').hide();
            }
            $("#open-tag-collapse").on("click", function () {
                openTagToggle($("#open-tag")[0]);
            });
        });

!function(){    var $ = require('wiki-common:widget/lib/jquery/jquery');
    var Dialog = require("wiki-common:widget/ui/dialog/dialog");
    var userLogin = require('wiki-common:widget/component/userLogin/userLogin');
    var unameFiller = require('wiki-common:widget/component/unameFiller/unameFiller');
    var rightCheck = require('wiki-lemma:widget/tools/rightCheck/rightCheck');
    var nsLog = require('wiki-common:widget/component/nslog/nslog');

            var isEnterprise = false;
        var enterpriseOwnerUserId = 0;
    
    var userId = 0;
    var editUrl = '/edit/' + encodeURIComponent('') + '/' + '7254372';
    var pgcUrl = '/enterprise/editpgc?lemmaId=7254372';
    var canDiscussion = $('.j-discussion-link').length > 0 ? true : false;

    userLogin.regist({
        onLogin: function(user) {
            userId = user ? user.uid : 0;
        }
    });

    function gotoEdit(url, isMidNight) {
        if (isMidNight) {
            Dialog.alert({
                title: '',
                subMsg: '23:008:00',
                onConfirm: function() {
                    window.location.href = url;
                }
            });
        } else {
            window.location.href = url;
        }    
    }

    function showChoseEditDialog(pgcCallback, ugcCallback) {
        new Dialog({
            title: '',
            subMsg: '<p></p><p><p>',
            btns: [{
            key: 'pgc',
            text: ''
            }, {
            style: 'white',
            text: '',
            key: 'ugc'
            }],
            onBtnClick: function(btnKey){
                if (btnKey === 'pgc') {
                    pgcCallback && pgcCallback();
                } else if (btnKey === 'ugc') {
                    ugcCallback && ugcCallback();
                }
            }
        }).show();
    }

    function checkUserLegal(res) {
        var legal = false;
        switch (res.errno) {
            case 100001:
                nsLog('10003106');
                userLogin.showLoginPop();
                break;
            case 100006:
                unameFiller.show();
                break;
            default:
                legal = true;
        }
        return true;
    }

    function checkUgc(res, url) {
        if (res.errno) {
            switch (res.errno) {
                case 100005:
                    alert('');
                    break;
                case 110001:
                    alert('');
                    break;
                case 110007:
                    alert('');
                    break;
                case 110005:
                    nsLog('10003101');
                    var content = '<div style="text-align: left;width: 490px">'
                        + '<h2 style="font-size: 20px;color: #333;line-height: 26px;margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 20px;">' 
                        + '</h2>' 
                        + '<p style="font-size: 16px;color: #333;line-height: 26px;margin-bottom: 17px;">'
                        + '485%</p>'
                        + '<p style="font-size: 16px;color: #333">'
                        + res.data.userInfo.level + ''
                        + res.data.userInfo.passRatio + '%</p></div>';
                    var btns = [
                        {
                            key: 'join',
                            text: '<span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: center;vertical-align: middle;display: table-cell;"></span>'
                        },
                        {
                            text: '<span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: center;vertical-align: middle;display: table-cell;"></span>',
                            key: 'task'
                        }
                    ];
                    if (canDiscussion) {
                        btns = [
                            {
                                key: 'discussion',
                                text: '<span style="font-size: 14px"></span>'
                            },
                            {
                                text: '<span style="font-size: 14px"></span>',
                                key: 'task'
                            }
                        ];
                    }
                    new Dialog({
                        title: '',
                        content: content,
                        btns: btns,
                        onBtnClick: function(btnKey){
                            if (btnKey === 'discussion') {
                                window.location.href = '/planet/talk?lemmaId=7254372&category=1';
                            } else if (btnKey === 'task') {
                                window.location.href = '/usercenter#guide';
                            } else if (btnKey === 'join') {
                                window.location.href = '/feedback';
                            }
                        }
                    }).show();
                    break;
                case 110008:
                    nsLog('10003102');
                    var content = '<div style="text-align: left;width: 490px">'
                        + '<h2 style="font-size: 20px;color: #333;line-height: 26px;margin-bottom: 20px;margin-top: 10px;">' 
                        + '</h2>' 
                        + '<p style="font-size: 16px;color: #333;line-height: 26px;margin-bottom: 17px;">'
                        + '685%</p>'
                        + '<p style="font-size: 16px;color: #333">'
                        + res.data.userInfo.level + ''
                        + res.data.userInfo.passRatio + '%</p></div>';
                    var btns = [
                        {
                            key: 'join',
                            text: '<span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: center;vertical-align: middle;display: table-cell;"></span>'
                        },
                        {
                            text: '<span style="font-size: 14px;text-align: center;vertical-align: middle;display: table-cell;"></span>',
                            key: 'task'
                        }
                    ];
                    if (canDiscussion) {
                        btns = [
                            {
                                key: 'discussion',
                                text: '<span style="font-size: 14px"></span>'
                            },
                            {
                                text: '<span style="font-size: 14px"></span>',
                                key: 'task'
                            }
                        ];
                    }
                    new Dialog({
                        title: '',
                        content: content,
                        btns: btns,
                        onBtnClick: function(btnKey){
                            if (btnKey === 'discussion') {
                                window.location.href = '/planet/talk?lemmaId=7254372&category=1';
                            } else if (btnKey === 'task') {
                                window.location.href = '/usercenter#guide';
                            } else if (btnKey === 'join') {
                                window.location.href = '/feedback';
                            }
                        }
                    }).show();
                    break;
                case 470001:
                    alert('');
                    break;
                case 110003:
                    nsLog('10003103');
                    Dialog.alert({
                        title: '',
                        subMsg: '<br/>'
                    });
                    break;
            }
        } else {
            if (!res.data.right.noAudit) {
                Dialog.alert({
                    title: '',
                    subMsg: '<br/>'
                });
                return;
            }
            gotoEdit(url, res.data.notice.isMidNight);
        }
    }

    $(document.body).on('click', '.j-edit-link', function() {
        nsLog('10003100');
        var dl = $(this).attr('data-edit-dl');
        if (dl) {
            var url = editUrl + '?dl=' + dl;
        } else {
            var url = editUrl;
        }

        rightCheck.preeditCheck('7254372', '', '', '134256741', '', function(res) {
            if (!checkUserLegal(res)) {
                return;
            }
            if (isEnterprise && enterpriseOwnerUserId === userId) {
                showChoseEditDialog(function() {
                    location.href = pgcUrl;
                }, function() {
                    checkUgc(res, url);
                });
            } else {
                checkUgc(res, url);
            }
        });
    });
}();

!function(){    var $ = require('wiki-common:widget/lib/jquery/jquery'),
      animation = require('wiki-common:widget/util/animation'),
      nslog = require('wiki-common:widget/component/nslog/nslog'),
      initSearchbar = require('wiki-common:widget/component/searchbar/searchbar');

    var isFadeIn = false,
        isFadeOut = false;

    var fadeInAni, fadeOutAni;

    $(window).on('scroll', function(e) {
        var scrollTop = $(this).scrollTop();

        if (scrollTop > 200 && !isFadeIn && $('.lemmaWgt-searchHeader').css('display') == 'none') {
            fadeOutAni && fadeOutAni.stop();
            fadeInAni = animation({
                duration: 200,
                easing: 'linear',
                onStart: function() {
                    isFadeOut = false;
                    isFadeIn = true;
                    $('.lemmaWgt-searchHeader').css('display', 'block');
                },
                onStep: function(progress) {
                    $('.lemmaWgt-searchHeader').css('opacity', progress)
                },
                onComplete: function(progress) {
                    isFadeIn = false;
                    nslog(10010007);
                }
            });
        } else if (scrollTop <= 200 && !isFadeOut && $('.lemmaWgt-searchHeader').css('display') == 'block') {
            fadeInAni && fadeInAni.stop();
            fadeOutAni = animation({
                duration: 300,
                easing: 'linear',
                onStart: function() {
                    $('.lemmaWgt-searchHeader #suggestion').hide();
                    isFadeIn = false;
                    isFadeOut = true;
                },
                onStep: function(progress) {
                    $('.lemmaWgt-searchHeader').css('opacity', 1 - progress);
                },
                onComplete: function(progress) {
                    isFadeOut = false;
                    $('.lemmaWgt-searchHeader').css('display', 'none');
                }
            });
        }
    });
}();
